<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Chinese_language" title="Chinese language">Chinese</a>: <span lang="zh"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E6%88%90%E5%90%89%E6%80%9D%E6%B1%97" title="wikt:成吉思汗">成吉思汗</a></span>; <a href="/wiki/Pinyin" title="Pinyin">pinyin</a>: <i><span lang="zh-Latn-pinyin">Chéngjísī Hán</span></i>; <a href="/wiki/Wade%E2%80%93Giles" title="Wade–Giles">Wade–Giles</a>: <i><span lang="zh-Latn-wadegile">Ch'eng<sup>2</sup>-chi<sup>2</sup>-szu<sup>1</sup> Han<sup>4</sup></span></i>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-11">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Historians of the Mongol empire generally prefer the spelling <b>Chingis Khan</b> or <b>Chinggis Khan</b>, which more closely approximates the name in <a href="/wiki/Mongolian_language" title="Mongolian language">Mongolian</a>, <span title="Mongolian-language text"><span lang="mn">Чингис хаан</span></span> <small></small><span class="IPA" lang="mn-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Mongolian" title="Help:IPA/Mongolian">[t͡ʃʰiŋɡɪs xaːŋ]</a></span>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEMorgan1986186_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEMorgan1986186-9">[7]</a></sup> The English spelling of his name came originally from <a href="/wiki/Italian_language" title="Italian language">Italian</a>, hence the pronunciation <span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt" lang="en-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ˌ/: secondary stress follows">ˌ</span><span title="/dʒ/: 'j' in 'jam'">dʒ</span><span title="/ɛ/: 'e' in 'dress'">ɛ</span><span title="/ŋ/: 'ng' in 'sing'">ŋ</span><span title="/ɡ/: 'g' in 'guy'">ɡ</span><span title="/ɪ/: 'i' in 'kit'">ɪ</span><span title="'s' in 'sigh'">s</span></span><span class="wrap"> </span><span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'k' in 'kind'">k</span><span title="/ɑː/: 'a' in 'father'">ɑː</span><span title="'n' in 'nigh'">n</span></span>/</a></span></span>, which is similar to the Italian pronunciation; the second <i>G</i> has a following <i>H</i> to produce the sound <small></small><span class="IPA" lang="it-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Italian" title="Help:IPA/Italian">[g]</a></span>, as in <i>spaghetti</i>. But because <i>G</i> before <i>E</i> in English is ambiguous (cf. <i>get</i> vs. <i>gel</i>), this leads to the common pronunciation of <span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt" lang="en-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ˌ/: secondary stress follows">ˌ</span><span title="/ɡ/: 'g' in 'guy'">ɡ</span><span title="/ɛ/: 'e' in 'dress'">ɛ</span><span title="/ŋ/: 'ng' in 'sing'">ŋ</span><span title="/ɡ/: 'g' in 'guy'">ɡ</span><span title="/ɪ/: 'i' in 'kit'">ɪ</span><span title="'s' in 'sigh'">s</span></span><span class="wrap"> </span><span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'k' in 'kind'">k</span><span title="/ɑː/: 'a' in 'father'">ɑː</span><span title="'n' in 'nigh'">n</span></span>/</a></span></span>, with both <i>G</i>s producing the sound <span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt" lang="en-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ɡ/: 'g' in 'guy'">ɡ</span></span>/</a></span></span>, which has led to the alternative spelling <i>Jenghis Khan</i> to try to prevent this.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[8]</a></sup> The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Middle_Mongol_language" title="Middle Mongol language">Middle Mongol</a> pronunciation was <small></small><span class="IPA" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA" title="Help:IPA">[ˈt͡ɕʰiŋːɡis ˈkaχaːn]</a></span> or <small></small><span class="IPA" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA" title="Help:IPA">[ˈt͡ʃʰiŋːɡis ˈqaχaːn]</a></span>.</span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>

</div></td></tr></tbody></table><div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div></div></td></tr><tr><td class="navbox-list navbox-odd hlist" colspan="2" style="width:100%;padding:0"><div style="padding:0 0.25em"></div><table class="nowraplinks mw-collapsible mw-collapsed navbox-subgroup" style="border-spacing:0"><tbody><tr><th class="navbox-title" colspan="2" scope="col"><div id="People" style="font-size:114%;margin:0 4em">People</div></th></tr><tr><td class="navbox-list navbox-odd" colspan="2" style="width:100%;padding:0"><div style="padding:0 0.25em"></div><table class="nowraplinks navbox-subgroup" style="border-spacing:0"><tbody><tr><th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="width:1%"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Mongol_Khans" title="List of Mongol Khans">Great Khans</a></th><td class="navbox-list-with-group navbox-list navbox-odd" style="width:100%;padding:0"><div style="padding:0 0.25em">

<div class="navbox-styles nomobile"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1061467846" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/></div><div aria-labelledby="Khagan-Emperors_of_the_Yuan_dynasty" class="navbox" role="navigation" style="padding:3px"><table class="nowraplinks mw-collapsible autocollapse navbox-inner" style="border-spacing:0;background:transparent;color:inherit"><tbody><tr><th class="navbox-title" colspan="3" scope="col"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1063604349" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="navbar plainlinks hlist navbar-mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Yuan_emperors" title="Template:Yuan emperors"><abbr style=";;background:none transparent;border:none;box-shadow:none;padding:0;" title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Yuan_emperors" title="Template talk:Yuan emperors"><abbr style=";;background:none transparent;border:none;box-shadow:none;padding:0;" title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Yuan_emperors&amp;action=edit"><abbr style=";;background:none transparent;border:none;box-shadow:none;padding:0;" title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div><div id="Khagan-Emperors_of_the_Yuan_dynasty" style="font-size:114%;margin:0 4em"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_emperors_of_the_Yuan_dynasty" title="List of emperors of the Yuan dynasty">Khagan-Emperors</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Yuan_dynasty" title="Yuan dynasty">Yuan dynasty</a></div></th></tr><tr><th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="width:1%"><a href="/wiki/Yuan_dynasty" title="Yuan dynasty">Yuan</a></th><td class="navbox-list-with-group navbox-list navbox-odd hlist" style="width:100%;padding:0"><div style="padding:0 0.25em"><span style="font-size:85%;"><b>Early Mongol rulers posthumously honoured by </b><a href="/wiki/Kublai_Khan" title="Kublai Khan">Kublai</a><b> as Yuan emperors</b></span>
<ul><li><a class="mw-selflink selflink">Taizu</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tolui" title="Tolui">Ruizong</a> (regent)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%C3%96gedei_Khan" title="Ögedei Khan">Taizong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/G%C3%BCy%C3%BCk_Khan" title="Güyük Khan">Dingzong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/M%C3%B6ngke_Khan" title="Möngke Khan">Xianzong</a></li></ul>
<p><span style="font-size:85%;"><b>Following Kublai's enthronement as <a href="/wiki/Khagan" title="Khagan">Khagan</a>-<a href="/wiki/Emperor_of_China" title="Emperor of China">Emperor</a> in 1260, proclamation of the dynastic name "Great Yuan" in 1271, and <a href="/wiki/Mongol_conquest_of_the_Song_dynasty" title="Mongol conquest of the Song dynasty">conquest</a> of <a href="/wiki/Song_dynasty" title="Song dynasty">Southern Song</a> in 1279, Yuan ruled all of China.</b></span>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Kublai_Khan" title="Kublai Khan">Shizu</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tem%C3%BCr_Khan" title="Temür Khan">Chengzong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/K%C3%BCl%C3%BCg_Khan" title="Külüg Khan">Wuzong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ayurbarwada_Buyantu_Khan" title="Ayurbarwada Buyantu Khan">Renzong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gegeen_Khan" title="Gegeen Khan">Yingzong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yes%C3%BCn_Tem%C3%BCr_(Yuan_dynasty)" title="Yesün Temür (Yuan dynasty)">Taiding Emperor</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ragibagh_Khan" title="Ragibagh Khan">Tianshun Emperor</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jayaatu_Khan_Tugh_Tem%C3%BCr" title="Jayaatu Khan Tugh Temür">Wenzong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Khutughtu_Khan_Kusala" title="Khutughtu Khan Kusala">Mingzong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rinchinbal_Khan" title="Rinchinbal Khan">Ningzong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Toghon_Tem%C3%BCr" title="Toghon Temür">Huizong (Emperor Shun)</a></li></ul></div></td><td class="noviewer navbox-image" rowspan="2" style="width:1px;padding:0 0 0 2px"><div><span style="font-size:36px;">元</span></div></td></tr><tr><th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="width:1%"><a href="/wiki/Northern_Yuan" title="Northern Yuan">Northern Yuan</a></th><td class="navbox-list-with-group navbox-list navbox-even hlist" style="width:100%;padding:0"><div style="padding:0 0.25em">
<li><a href="/wiki/Toghon_Tem%C3%BCr" title="Toghon Temür">Huizong (Emperor Shun)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Biligt%C3%BC_Khan_Ayushiridara" title="Biligtü Khan Ayushiridara">Zhaozong</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Uskhal_Khan_T%C3%B6g%C3%BCs_Tem%C3%BCr" title="Uskhal Khan Tögüs Temür">Tianyuan Emperor</a></li>
</div></td></tr><tr><td class="navbox-abovebelow" colspan="3"><div><span style="font-size:85%;"><b>Note:</b> Before <a href="/wiki/Kublai_Khan" title="Kublai Khan">Kublai</a> announced the dynastic name "<a href="/wiki/Yuan_dynasty" title="Yuan dynasty">Great Yuan</a>" in 1271, <a href="/wiki/Khagan" title="Khagan">Khagans</a> (Great Khans) of the "Great Mongol State" (<i>Ikh Mongol Uls</i>) already started to use the Chinese title of <a href="/wiki/Emperor_of_China" title="Emperor of China">Emperor</a> (<a href="/wiki/Chinese_language" title="Chinese language">Chinese</a>: <span lang="zh">皇帝</span>; <a href="/wiki/Pinyin" title="Pinyin">pinyin</a>: <i><span lang="zh-Latn-pinyin">Huángdì</span></i>) practically in the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_language" title="Chinese language">Chinese language</a> since the enthronement of <a class="mw-selflink selflink">Genghis Emperor</a> (<span lang="zh">成吉思皇帝</span>) in 1206.</span>
